Only used by the SOCKS GSSAPI functions.\n    91→ */\n    92→int Curl_blockread_all(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\n    93→                       struct Curl_easy *data,   /* transfer */\n    94→                       char *buf,                /* store read data here */\n    95→                       ssize_t buffersize,       /* max amount to read */\n    96→                       ssize_t *n)               /* amount bytes read */\n    97→{\n    98→  ssize_t nread = 0;\n    99→  ssize_t allread = 0;\n   100→  int result;\n   101→  CURLcode err = CURLE_OK;\n   102→\n   103→  *n = 0;\n   104→  for(;;) 259→  sx->outp += nread;\n   260→  return CURLPX_OK;\n   261→}\n   262→\n   263→/*\n   264→* This function logs in to a SOCKS4 proxy and sends the specifics to the final\n   265→* destination socks_state *sx,\n   276→                               struct Curl_easy *data)\n   277→{\n   278→  struct connectdata *conn = cf->conn;\n   279→  const bool protocol4a =\n   280→    (conn->socks_proxy.proxytype == CURLPROXY_SOCKS4A) ? TRUE : FALSE;\n   281→  unsigned char *socksreq = (unsigned char *)data->state.buffer;\n   282→  CURLcode result;\n   283→  CURLproxycode presult;\n   284→  struct Curl_dns_entry *dns = NULL;\n   285→\n   286→  /* make sure that the buffer is at least 600 bytes */\n   287→  DEBUGASSERT(READBUFFER_MIN >= 600);\n   288→\n   289→  switch(sx->state) {\n   290→  case CONNECT_SOCKS_INIT:\n   291→    /* SOCKS4 can only do IPv4, insist! */\n   292→    conn->ip_version = CURL_IPRESOLVE_V4;\n   293→    if(conn->bits.httpproxy)\n   294→      infof(data, \"SOCKS4%s: connecting to HTTP proxy %s port %d\",\n   295→            protocol4a ? \"a\" : \"\", sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\n   296→\n   297→    infof(data, \"SOCKS4 communication to %s:%d\",\n   298→          sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\n   299→\n   300→    /*\n   301→     * Compose socks4 request\n   302→     *\n   303→     * Request format\n   304→     *\n   305→     *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+....+----+\n   306→     *     | VN | CD | DSTPORT |      DSTIP        | USERID       |NULL|\n   307→     *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+....+----+\n   308→     * # of bytes:  1    1      2              4           variable       1\n   309→     */\n   310→\n   311→    socksreq[0] = 4; /* version (SOCKS4) */\n   312→    socksreq[1] = 1; /* connect */\n   313→    socksreq[2] = (unsigned char)((sx->remote_port >> 8) & 0xff); /* MSB */\n   314→    socksreq[3] = (unsigned char)(sx->remote_port & 0xff);        /* LSB */\n   315→\n   316→    /* DNS resolve only for SOCKS4, not SOCKS4a */\n   317→    if(!protocol4a) {\n   318→      enum resolve_t rc =\n   319→        Curl_resolv(data, sx->hostname, sx->remote_port, TRUE, &dns);\n   320→\n   321→      if(rc == CURLRESOLV_ERROR)\n   322→        return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\n   323→      else if(rc == CURLRESOLV_PENDING) {\n   324→        sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVING);\n   325→        infof(data, \"SOCKS4 non-blocking resolve of %s\", sx->hostname);\n   326→        return CURLPX_OK;\n   327→      }\n   328→      sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVED);\n   329→      goto CONNECT_RESOLVED;\n   330→    }\n   331→\n   332→    /* socks4a doesn't resolve anything locally */\n   333→    sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_INIT);\n   334→    goto CONNECT_REQ_INIT;\n   335→\n   336→  case CONNECT_RESOLVING:\n   337→    /* check if we have the name resolved by now */\n   338→    dns = Curl_fetch_addr(data, sx->hostname, (int)conn->port);\n   339→\n   340→    if(dns) {\n   341→#ifdef CURLRES_ASYNCH\n   342→      data->state.async.dns = dns;\n   343→      data->state.async.done = TRUE;\n   344→#endif\n   345→      infof(data, \"Hostname '%s' was found\", sx->hostname);\n   346→      sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVED);\n   347→    }\n   348→    else {\n   349→      result = Curl_resolv_check(data, &dns);\n   350→      if(!dns) {\n   351→        if(result)\n   352→          return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\n   353→        return CURLPX_OK;\n   354→      }\n   355→    }\n   356→    /* FALLTHROUGH */\n   357→CONNECT_RESOLVED:\n   358→  case CONNECT_RESOLVED: {\n   359→    struct Curl_addrinfo *hp = NULL;\n   360→    /*\n   361→     * We cannot use 'hostent' as a struct that Curl_resolv() returns.  It\n   362→     * returns a Curl_addrinfo pointer that may not always look the same.\n   363→     */\n   364→    if(dns) {\n   365→      hp = dns->addr;\n   366→\n   367→      /* scan for the first IPv4 address */\n   368→      while(hp && (hp->ai_family != AF_INET))\n   369→        hp = hp->ai_next;\n   370→\n   371→      if(hp) {\n   372→        struct sockaddr_in *saddr_in;\n   373→        char buf[64];\n   374→        Curl_printable_address(hp, buf, sizeof(buf));\n   375→\n   376→        saddr_in = (struct sockaddr_in *)(void *)hp->ai_addr;\n   377→        socksreq[4] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[0];\n   378→        socksreq[5] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[1];\n   379→        socksreq[6] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[2];\n   380→        socksreq[7] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[3];\n   381→\n   382→        infof(data, \"SOCKS4 connect to IPv4 %s (locally resolved)\", buf);\n   383→\n   384→        Curl_resolv_unlock(data, dns); /* not used anymore from now on */\n   385→      }\n   386→      else\n   387→        failf(data, \"SOCKS4 connection to %s not supported\", sx->hostname);\n   388→    }\n   389→    else\n   390→      failf(data, \"Failed to resolve \\\"%s\\\" for SOCKS4 connect.\",\n   391→            sx->hostname);\n   392→\n   393→    if(!hp)\n   394→      return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\n   395→  }\n   396→    /* FALLTHROUGH */\n   397→CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\n   398→  case CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\n   399→    /*\n   400→     * This is currently not supporting \"Identification Protocol (RFC1413)\".\n   401→     */\n   402→    socksreq[8] = 0; /* ensure empty userid is NUL-terminated */\n   403→    if(sx->proxy_user) {\n   404→      size_t plen = strlen(sx->proxy_user);\n   405→      if(plen >= (size_t)data->set.buffer_size - 8) {\n   406→        failf(data, \"Too long SOCKS proxy user name, can't use\");\n   407→        return CURLPX_LONG_USER;\n   408→      }\n   409→      /* copy the proxy name WITH trailing zero */\n   410→      memcpy(socksreq + 8, sx->proxy_user, plen + 1);\n   411→    }\n   412→\n   413→    /*\n   414→     * Make connection\n   415→     */\n   416→    {\n   417→      size_t packetsize = 9 +\n   418→        strlen((char *)socksreq + 8); /* size including NUL */\n   419→\n   420→      /* If SOCKS4a, set special invalid IP address 0.0.0.x */\n   421→      if(protocol4a) {\n   422→        size_t hostnamelen = 0;\n   423→        socksreq[4] = 0;\n   424→        socksreq[5] = 0;\n   425→        socksreq[6] = 0;\n   426→        socksreq[7] = 1;\n   427→        /* append hostname */\n   428→        hostnamelen = strlen(sx->hostname) + 1; /* length including NUL */\n   429→        if(hostnamelen <= 255)\n   430→          strcpy((char *)socksreq + packetsize, sx->hostname);\n   431→        else {\n   432→          failf(data, \"SOCKS4: too long host name\");\n   433→          return CURLPX_LONG_HOSTNAME;\n   434→        }\n   435→        packetsize += hostnamelen;\n   436→      }\n   437→      sx->outp = socksreq;\n   438→      sx->outstanding = packetsize;\n   439→      sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_SENDING);\n   440→    }\n   441→    /* FALLTHROUGH */\n   442→  case CONNECT_REQ_SENDING:\n   443→    /* Send request */\n   444→    presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_CONNECT,\n   445→                               \"SOCKS4 connect request\");\n   446→    if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n   447→      return presult;\n   448→    else if(sx->outstanding) {\n   449→      /* remain in sending state */\n   450→      return CURLPX_OK;\n   451→    }\n   452→    /* done sending! */\n   453→    sx->outstanding = 8; /* receive data size */\n   454→    sx->outp = socksreq;\n   455→    sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_SOCKS_READ);\n   456→\n   457→    /* FALLTHROUGH */\n   458→  case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ:\n   459→    /* Receive response */\n   460→    presult = socks_state_recv(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_RECV_CONNECT,\n   461→                               \"connect request ack\");\n   462→    if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n   463→      return presult;\n   464→    else if(sx->outstanding) {\n   465→      /* remain in reading state */\n   466→      return CURLPX_OK;\n   467→    }\n   468→    sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_DONE);\n   469→    break;\n   470→  default: /* lots of unused states in SOCKS4 */\n   471→    break;\n   472→  }\n   473→\n   474→  /*\n   475→   * Response format\n   476→   *\n   477→   *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+\n   478→   *     | VN | CD | DSTPORT |      DSTIP        |\n   479→   *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+\n   480→   * # of bytes:  1    1      2              4\n   481→   *\n   482→   * VN is the version of the reply code and should be 0. CD is the result\n   483→   * code with one of the following values:\n   484→   *\n   485→   * 90: request granted\n   486→   * 91: request rejected or failed\n   487→   * 92: request rejected because SOCKS server cannot connect to\n   488→   *     identd on the client\n   489→   * 93: request rejected because the client program and identd\n   490→   *     report different user-ids\n   491→   */\n   492→\n   493→  /* wrong version ? */\n   494→  if(socksreq[0]) {\n   495→    failf(data,\n   496→          \"SOCKS4 reply has wrong version, version should be 0.\");\n   497→    return CURLPX_BAD_VERSION;\n   498→  }\n   499→\n   500→  /* Result */\n   501→  switch(socksreq[1]) {\n   502→  case 90:\n   503→    infof(data, \"SOCKS4%s request granted.\", protocol4a?\"a\":\"\");\n   504→    break;\n   505→  case 91:\n   506→    failf(data,\n   507→          \"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\"\n   508→          \", request rejected or failed.\",\n   509→          socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\n   510→          (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\n   511→          (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\n   512→    return CURLPX_REQUEST_FAILED;\n   513→  case 92:\n   514→    failf(data,\n   515→          \"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\"\n   516→          \", request rejected because SOCKS server cannot connect to \"\n   517→          \"identd on the client.\",\n   518→          socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\n   519→          (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\n   520→          (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\n   521→    return CURLPX_IDENTD;\n   522→  case 93:\n   523→    failf(data,\n   524→          \"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\"\n   525→          \", request rejected because the client program and identd \"\n   526→          \"report different user-ids.\",\n   527→          socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\n   528→          (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\n   529→          (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\n   530→    return CURLPX_IDENTD_DIFFER;\n   531→  default:\n   532→    failf(data,\n   533→          \"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\"\n   534→          \", Unknown.\",\n   535→          socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\n   536→          (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\n   537→          (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\n   538→    return CURLPX_UNKNOWN_FAIL;\n   539→  }\n   540→\n   541→  return CURLPX_OK; /* Proxy was successful! */\n   542→}\n   543→\n   544→/*\n   545→ * This function logs in to a SOCKS5 proxy and sends the specifics to the final\n   546→ * destination server.\n   547→ */\n   548→static CURLproxycode do_SOCKS5(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\n   549→                               struct socks_state *sx,\n   550→                               struct Curl_easy *data)\n   551→{\n   552→  /*\n   553→    According to the RFC1928, section \"6.  Replies\". This is what a SOCK5\n   554→    replies:\n   555→\n   556→        +----+-----+-------+------+----------+----------+\n   557→        |VER | REP |  RSV  | ATYP | BND.ADDR | BND.PORT |\n   558→        +----+-----+-------+------+----------+----------+\n   559→        | 1  |  1  | X'00' |  1   | Variable |    2     |\n   560→        +----+-----+-------+------+----------+----------+\n   561→\n   562→    Where:\n   563→\n   564→    o  VER    protocol version: X'05'\n   565→    o  REP    Reply field:\n   566→    o  X'00' succeeded\n   567→  */\n   568→  struct connectdata *conn = cf->conn;\n   569→  unsigned char *socksreq = (unsigned char *)data->state.buffer;\n   570→  int idx;\n   571→  CURLcode result;\n   572→  CURLproxycode presult;\n   573→  bool socks5_resolve_local =\n   574→    (conn->socks_proxy.proxytype == CURLPROXY_SOCKS5) ? TRUE : FALSE;\n   575→  const size_t hostname_len = strlen(sx->hostname);\n   576→  ssize_t len = 0;\n   577→  const unsigned char auth = data->set.socks5auth;\n   578→  bool allow_gssapi = FALSE;\n   579→  struct Curl_dns_entry *dns = NULL;\n   580→\n   581→  DEBUGASSERT(auth & (CURLAUTH_BASIC | CURLAUTH_GSSAPI));\n   582→  switch(sx->state) {\n   583→  case CONNECT_SOCKS_INIT:\n   584→    if(conn->bits.httpproxy)\n   585→      infof(data, \"SOCKS5: connecting to HTTP proxy %s port %d\",\n   586→            sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\n   587→\n   588→    /* RFC1928 chapter 5 specifies max 255 chars for domain name in packet */\n   589→    if(!socks5_resolve_local && hostname_len > 255) {\n   590→      infof(data, \"SOCKS5: server resolving disabled for hostnames of \"\n   591→            \"length > 255 [actual len=%zu]\", hostname_len);\n   592→      socks5_resolve_local = TRUE;\n   593→    }\n   594→\n   595→    if(auth & ~(CURLAUTH_BASIC | CURLAUTH_GSSAPI))\n   596→      infof(data,\n   597→            \"warning: unsupported value passed to CURLOPT_SOCKS5_AUTH: %u\",\n   598→            auth);\n   599→    if(!(auth & CURLAUTH_BASIC))\n   600→      /* disable username/password auth */\n   601→      sx->proxy_user = NULL;\n   602→#if defined(HAVE_GSSAPI) || defined(USE_WINDOWS_SSPI)\n   603→    if(auth & CURLAUTH_GSSAPI)\n   604→      allow_gssapi = TRUE;\n   605→#endif\n   606→\n   607→    idx = 0;\n   608→    socksreq[idx++] = 5;   /* version */\n   609→    idx++;                 /* number of authentication methods */\n   610→    socksreq[idx++] = 0;   /* no authentication */\n   611→    if(allow_gssapi)\n   612→      socksreq[idx++] = 1; /* GSS-API */\n   613→    if(sx->proxy_user)\n   614→      socksreq[idx++] = 2; /* username/password */\n   615→    /* write the number of authentication methods */\n   616→    socksreq[1] = (unsigned char) (idx - 2);\n   617→\n   618→    sx->outp = socksreq;\n   619→    sx->outstanding = idx;\n   620→    presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_CONNECT,\n   621→                               \"initial SOCKS5 request\");\n   622→    if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n   623→      return presult;\n   624→    else if(sx->outstanding) {\n   625→      /* remain in sending state */\n   626→      return CURLPX_OK;\n   627→    }\n   628→    sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_SOCKS_READ);\n   629→    goto CONNECT_SOCKS_READ_INIT;\n   630→  case CONNECT_SOCKS_SEND:\n   631→    presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_CONNECT,\n   632→                               \"initial SOCKS5 request\");\n   633→    if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n   634→      return presult;\n   635→    else if(sx->outstanding) {\n   636→      /* remain in sending state */\n   637→      return CURLPX_OK;\n   638→    }\n   639→    /* FALLTHROUGH */\n   640→CONNECT_SOCKS_READ_INIT:\n   641→  case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ_INIT:\n   642→    sx->outstanding = 2; /* expect two bytes */\n   643→    sx->outp = socksreq; /* store it here */\n   644→    /* FALLTHROUGH */\n   645→  case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ:\n   646→    presult = socks_state_recv(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_RECV_CONNECT,\n   647→                               \"initial SOCKS5 response\");\n   648→    if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n   649→      return presult;\n   650→    else if(sx->outstanding) {\n   651→      /* remain in reading state */\n   652→      return CURLPX_OK;\n   653→    }\n   654→    else if(socksreq[0] != 5) {\n   655→      failf(data, \"Received invalid version in initial SOCKS5 response.\");\n   656→      return CURLPX_BAD_VERSION;\n   657→    }\n   658→    else if(socksreq[1] == 0) {\n   659→      /* DONE! No authentication needed. Send request. */\n   660→      sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_INIT);\n   661→      goto CONNECT_REQ_INIT;\n   662→    }\n   663→    else if(socksreq[1] == 2) {\n   664→      /* regular name + password authentication */\n   665→      sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_AUTH_INIT);\n   666→      goto CONNECT_AUTH_INIT;\n   667→    }\n   668→#if defined(HAVE_GSSAPI) || defined(USE_WINDOWS_SSPI)\n   669→    else if(allow_gssapi && (socksreq[1] == 1)) {\n   670→      sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_GSSAPI_INIT);\n   671→      result = Curl_SOCKS5_gssapi_negotiate(cf, data);\n   672→      if(result) {\n   673→        failf(data, \"Unable to negotiate SOCKS5 GSS-API context.\");\n   674→        return CURLPX_GSSAPI;\n   675→      }\n   676→    }\n   677→#endif\n   678→    else {\n   679→      /* error */\n   680→      if(!allow_gssapi && (socksreq[1] == 1)) {\n   681→        failf(data,\n   682→              \"SOCKS5 GSSAPI per-message authentication is not supported.\");\n   683→        return CURLPX_GSSAPI_PERMSG;\n   684→      }\n   685→      else if(socksreq[1] == 255) {\n   686→        failf(data, \"No authentication method was acceptable.\");\n   687→        return CURLPX_NO_AUTH;\n   688→      }\n   689→    }\n   690→    failf(data,\n   691→          \"Undocumented SOCKS5 mode attempted to be used by server.\");\n   692→    return CURLPX_UNKNOWN_MODE;\n   693→#if defined(HAVE_GSSAPI) || defined(USE_WINDOWS_SSPI)\n   694→  case CONNECT_GSSAPI_INIT:\n   695→    /* GSSAPI stuff done non-blocking */\n   696→    break;\n   697→#endif\n   698→\n   699→  default: /* do nothing! */\n   700→    break;\n   701→\n   702→CONNECT_AUTH_INIT:\n   703→  case CONNECT_AUTH_INIT: {\n   704→    /* Needs user name and password */\n   705→    size_t proxy_user_len, proxy_password_len;\n   706→    if(sx->proxy_user && sx->proxy_password) {\n   707→      proxy_user_len = strlen(sx->proxy_user);\n   708→      proxy_password_len = strlen(sx->proxy_password);\n   709→    }\n   710→    else {\n   711→      proxy_user_len = 0;\n   712→      proxy_password_len = 0;\n   713→    }\n   714→\n   715→    /*   username/password request looks like\n   716→     * +----+------+----------+------+----------+\n   717→     * |VER | ULEN |  UNAME   | PLEN |  PASSWD  |\n   718→     * +----+------+----------+------+----------+\n   719→     * | 1  |  1   | 1 to 255 |  1   | 1 to 255 |\n   720→     * +----+------+----------+------+----------+\n   721→     */\n   722→    len = 0;\n   723→    socksreq[len++] = 1;    /* username/pw subnegotiation version */\n   724→    socksreq[len++] = (unsigned char) proxy_user_len;\n   725→    if(sx->proxy_user && proxy_user_len) {\n   726→      /* the length must fit in a single byte */\n   727→      if(proxy_user_len > 255) {\n   728→        failf(data, \"Excessive user name length for proxy auth\");\n   729→        return CURLPX_LONG_USER;\n   730→      }\n   731→      memcpy(socksreq + len, sx->proxy_user, proxy_user_len);\n   732→    }\n   733→    len += proxy_user_len;\n   734→    socksreq[len++] = (unsigned char) proxy_password_len;\n   735→    if(sx->proxy_password && proxy_password_len) {\n   736→      /* the length must fit in a single byte */\n   737→      if(proxy_password_len > 255) {\n   738→        failf(data, \"Excessive password length for proxy auth\");\n   739→        return CURLPX_LONG_PASSWD;\n   740→      }\n   741→      memcpy(socksreq + len, sx->proxy_password, proxy_password_len);\n   742→    }\n   743→    len += proxy_password_len;\n   744→    sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_AUTH_SEND);\n   745→    sx->outstanding = len;\n   746→    sx->outp = socksreq;\n   747→  }\n   748→    /* FALLTHROUGH */\n   749→  case CONNECT_AUTH_SEND:\n   750→    presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_AUTH,\n   751→                               \"SOCKS5 sub-negotiation request\");\n   752→    if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n   753→      return presult;\n   754→    else if(sx->outstanding) {\n   755→      /* remain in sending state */\n   756→      return CURLPX_OK;\n   757→    }\n   758→    sx->outp = socksreq;\n   759→    sx->outstanding = 2;\n   760→    sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_AUTH_READ);\n   761→    /* FALLTHROUGH */\n   762→  case CONNECT_AUTH_READ:\n   763→    presult = socks_state_recv(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_RECV_AUTH,\n   764→                               \"SOCKS5 sub-negotiation response\");\n   765→    if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n   766→      return presult;\n   767→    else if(sx->outstanding) {\n   768→      /* remain in reading state */\n   769→      return CURLPX_OK;\n   770→    }\n   771→    /* ignore the first (VER) byte */\n   772→    else if(socksreq[1]) { /* status */\n   773→      failf(data, \"User was rejected by the SOCKS5 server (%d %d).\",\n   774→            socksreq[0], socksreq[1]);\n   775→      return CURLPX_USER_REJECTED;\n   776→    }\n   777→\n   778→    /* Everything is good so far, user was authenticated! */\n   779→    sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_INIT);\n   780→    /* FALLTHROUGH */\n   781→CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\n   782→  case CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\n   783→    if(socks5_resolve_local) {\n   784→      enum resolve_t rc = Curl_resolv(data, sx->hostname, sx->remote_port,\n   785→                                      TRUE, &dns);\n   786→\n   787→      if(rc == CURLRESOLV_ERROR)\n   788→        return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\n   789→\n   790→      if(rc == CURLRESOLV_PENDING) {\n   791→        sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVING);\n   792→        return CURLPX_OK;\n   793→      }\n   794→      sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVED);\n   795→      goto CONNECT_RESOLVED;\n   796→    }\n   797→    goto CONNECT_RESOLVE_REMOTE;\n   798→\n   799→  case CONNECT_RESOLVING:\n   800→    /* check if we have the name resolved by now */\n   801→    dns = Curl_fetch_addr(data, sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\n   802→\n   803→    if(dns) {\n   804→#ifdef CURLRES_ASYNCH\n   805→      data->state.async.dns = dns;\n   806→      data->state.async.done = TRUE;\n   807→#endif\n   808→      infof(data, \"SOCKS5: hostname '%s' found\", sx->hostname);\n   809→    }\n   810→\n   811→ nread = 0;\n  ssize_t allread = 0;\n  int result;\n  CURLcode err = CURLE_OK;\n\n  *n = 0;\n  for(;;) {\n    timediff_t timeout_ms = Curl_timeleft(data, NULL, TRUE);\n    if(timeout_ms < 0) {\n      /* we already got the timeout */\n      result = CURLE_OPERATION_TIMEDOUT;\n      break;\n    }\n    if(!timeout_ms)\n      timeout_ms = TIMEDIFF_T_MAX;\n    if(SOCKET_READABLE(cf->conn->sock[cf->sockindex], timeout_ms) <= 0) {\n      result = ~CURLE_OK;\n      break;\n    }\n    nread = Curl_conn_cf_recv(cf->next, data, buf, buffersize, &err);\n    if(nread <= 0) {\n      result = err;\n      if(CURLE_AGAIN == err)\n        continue;\n      if(err) {\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n\n    if(buffersize == nread) {\n      allread += nread;\n      *n = allread;\n      result = CURLE_OK;\n      break;\n    }\n    if(!nread) {\n      result = ~CURLE_OK;\n      break;\n    }\n\n    buffersize -= nread;\n    buf += nread;\n    allread += nread;\n  }\n  return result;\n}\n#endif\n\n#if defined(DEBUGBUILD) && !defined(CURL_DISABLE_VERBOSE_STRINGS)\n#define DEBUG_AND_VERBOSE\n#define sxstate(x,d,y) socksstate(x,d,y, __LINE__)\n#else\n#define sxstate(x,d,y) socksstate(x,d,y)\n#endif\n\n/* always use this function to change state, to make debugging easier */\nstatic void socksstate(struct socks_state *sx, struct Curl_easy *data,\n                       enum connect_t state\n#ifdef DEBUG_AND_VERBOSE\n                       , int lineno\n#endif\n)\n{\n  enum connect_t oldstate = sx->state;\n#ifdef DEBUG_AND_VERBOSE\n  /* synced with the state list in urldata.h */\n  static const char * const socks_statename[] = {\n    \"INIT\",\n    \"SOCKS_INIT\",\n    \"SOCKS_SEND\",\n    \"SOCKS_READ_INIT\",\n    \"SOCKS_READ\",\n    \"GSSAPI_INIT\",\n    \"AUTH_INIT\",\n    \"AUTH_SEND\",\n    \"AUTH_READ\",\n    \"REQ_INIT\",\n    \"RESOLVING\",\n    \"RESOLVED\",\n    \"RESOLVE_REMOTE\",\n    \"REQ_SEND\",\n    \"REQ_SENDING\",\n    \"REQ_READ\",\n    \"REQ_READ_MORE\",\n    \"DONE\"\n  };\n#endif\n\n  (void)data;\n  if(oldstate == state)\n    /* don't bother when the new state is the same as the old state */\n    return;\n\n  sx->state = state;\n\n#ifdef DEBUG_AND_VERBOSE\n  infof(data,\n        \"SXSTATE: %s => %s; line %d\",\n        socks_statename[oldstate], socks_statename[sx->state],\n        lineno);\n#endif\n}\n\nstatic CURLproxycode socks_state_send(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\n                                      struct socks_state *sx,\n                                      struct Curl_easy *data,\n                                      CURLproxycode failcode,\n                                      const char *description)\n{\n  ssize_t nwritten;\n  CURLcode result;\n\n  nwritten = Curl_conn_cf_send(cf->next, data, (char *)sx->outp,\n                               sx->outstanding, &result);\n  if(nwritten <= 0) {\n    if(CURLE_AGAIN == result) {\n      return CURLPX_OK;\n    }\n    else if(CURLE_OK == result) {\n      /* connection closed */\n      failf(data, \"connection to proxy closed\");\n      return CURLPX_CLOSED;\n    }\n    failf(data, \"Failed to send %s: %s\", description,\n          curl_easy_strerror(result));\n    return failcode;\n  }\n  DEBUGASSERT(sx->outstanding >= nwritten);\n  /* not done, remain in state */\n  sx->outstanding -= nwritten;\n  sx->outp += nwritten;\n  return CURLPX_OK;\n}\n\nstatic CURLproxycode socks_state_recv(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\n                                      struct socks_state *sx,\n                                      struct Curl_easy *data,\n                                      CURLproxycode failcode,\n                                      const char *description)\n{\n  ssize_t nread;\n  CURLcode result;\n\n  nread = Curl_conn_cf_recv(cf->next, data, (char *)sx->outp,\n                            sx->outstanding, &result);\n  if(nread <= 0) {\n    if(CURLE_AGAIN == result) {\n      return CURLPX_OK;\n    }\n    else if(CURLE_OK == result) {\n      /* connection closed */\n      failf(data, \"connection to proxy closed\");\n      return CURLPX_CLOSED;\n    }\n    failf(data, \"SOCKS4: Failed receiving %s: %s\", description,\n          curl_easy_strerror(result));\n    return failcode;\n  }\n  /* remain in reading state */\n  DEBUGASSERT(sx->outstanding >= nread);\n  sx->outstanding -= nread;\n  sx->outp += nread;\n  return CURLPX_OK;\n}\n\n/*\n* This function logs in to a SOCKS4 proxy and sends the specifics to the final\n* destination server.\n*\n* Reference :\n*   https://www.openssh.com/txt/socks4.protocol\n*\n* Note :\n*   Set protocol4a=true for  \"SOCKS 4A (Simple Extension to SOCKS 4 Protocol)\"\n*   Nonsupport \"Identification Protocol (RFC1413)\"\n*/\nstatic CURLproxycode do_SOCKS4(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\n                               struct socks_state *sx,\n                               struct Curl_easy *data)\n{\n  struct connectdata *conn = cf->conn;\n  const bool protocol4a =\n    (conn->socks_proxy.proxytype == CURLPROXY_SOCKS4A) ? TRUE : FALSE;\n  unsigned char *socksreq = (unsigned char *)data->state.buffer;\n  CURLcode result;\n  CURLproxycode presult;\n  struct Curl_dns_entry *dns = NULL;\n\n  /* make sure that the buffer is at least 600 bytes */\n  DEBUGASSERT(READBUFFER_MIN >= 600);\n\n  switch(sx->state) {\n  case CONNECT_SOCKS_INIT:\n    /* SOCKS4 can only do IPv4, insist! */\n    conn->ip_version = CURL_IPRESOLVE_V4;\n    if(conn->bits.httpproxy)\n      infof(data, \"SOCKS4%s: connecting to HTTP proxy %s port %d\",\n            protocol4a ? \"a\" : \"\", sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\n\n    infof(data, \"SOCKS4 communication to %s:%d\",\n          sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\n\n    /*\n     * Compose socks4 request\n     *\n     * Request format\n     *\n     *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+....+----+\n     *     | VN | CD | DSTPORT |      DSTIP        | USERID       |NULL|\n     *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+....+----+\n     * # of bytes:  1    1      2              4           variable       1\n     */\n\n    socksreq[0] = 4; /* version (SOCKS4) */\n    socksreq[1] = 1; /* connect */\n    socksreq[2] = (unsigned char)((sx->remote_port >> 8) & 0xff); /* MSB */\n    socksreq[3] = (unsigned char)(sx->remote_port & 0xff);        /* LSB */\n\n    /* DNS resolve only for SOCKS4, not SOCKS4a */\n    if(!protocol4a) {\n      enum resolve_t rc =\n        Curl_resolv(data, sx->hostname, sx->remote_port, TRUE, &dns);\n\n      if(rc == CURLRESOLV_ERROR)\n        return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\n      else if(rc == CURLRESOLV_PENDING) {\n        sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVING);\n        infof(data, \"SOCKS4 non-blocking resolve of %s\", sx->hostname);\n        return CURLPX_OK;\n      }\n      sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVED);\n      goto CONNECT_RESOLVED;\n    }\n\n    /* socks4a doesn't resolve anything locally */\n    sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_INIT);\n    goto CONNECT_REQ_INIT;\n\n  case CONNECT_RESOLVING:\n    /* check if we have the name resolved by now */\n    dns = Curl_fetch_addr(data, sx->hostname, (int)conn->port);\n\n    if(dns) {\n#ifdef CURLRES_ASYNCH\n      data->state.async.dns = dns;\n      data->state.async.done = TRUE;\n#endif\n      infof(data, \"Hostname '%s' was found\", sx->hostname);\n      sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVED);\n    }\n    else {\n      result = Curl_resolv_check(data, &dns);\n      if(!dns) {\n        if(result)\n          return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\n        return CURLPX_OK;\n      }\n    }\n    /* FALLTHROUGH */\nCONNECT_RESOLVED:\n  case CONNECT_RESOLVED: {\n    struct Curl_addrinfo *hp = NULL;\n    /*\n     * We cannot use 'hostent' as a struct that Curl_resolv() returns.  It\n     * returns a Curl_addrinfo pointer that may not always look the same.\n     */\n    if(dns) {\n      hp = dns->addr;\n\n      /* scan for the first IPv4 address */\n      while(hp && (hp->ai_family != AF_INET))\n        hp = hp->ai_next;\n\n      if(hp) {\n        struct sockaddr_in *saddr_in;\n        char buf[64];\n        Curl_printable_address(hp, buf, sizeof(buf));\n\n        saddr_in = (struct sockaddr_in *)(void *)hp->ai_addr;\n        socksreq[4] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[0];\n        socksreq[5] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[1];\n        socksreq[6] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[2];\n        socksreq[7] = ((unsigned char *)&saddr_in->sin_addr.s_addr)[3];\n\n        infof(data, \"SOCKS4 connect to IPv4 %s (locally resolved)\", buf);\n\n        Curl_resolv_unlock(data, dns); /* not used anymore from now on */\n      }\n      else\n        failf(data, \"SOCKS4 connection to %s not supported\", sx->hostname);\n    }\n    else\n      failf(data, \"Failed to resolve \\\"%s\\\" for SOCKS4 connect.\",\n            sx->hostname);\n\n    if(!hp)\n      return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\n  }\n    /* FALLTHROUGH */\nCONNECT_REQ_INIT:\n  case CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\n    /*\n     * This is currently not supporting \"Identification Protocol (RFC1413)\".\n     */\n    socksreq[8] = 0; /* ensure empty userid is NUL-terminated */\n    if(sx->proxy_user) {\n      size_t plen = strlen(sx->proxy_user);\n      if(plen >= (size_t)data->set.buffer_size - 8) {\n        failf(data, \"Too long SOCKS proxy user name, can't use\");\n        return CURLPX_LONG_USER;\n      }\n      /* copy the proxy name WITH trailing zero */\n      memcpy(socksreq + 8, sx->proxy_user, plen + 1);\n    }\n\n    /*\n     * Make connection\n     */\n    {\n      size_t packetsize = 9 +\n        strlen((char *)socksreq + 8); /* size including NUL */\n\n      /* If SOCKS4a, set special invalid IP address 0.0.0.x */\n      if(protocol4a) {\n        size_t hostnamelen = 0;\n        socksreq[4] = 0;\n        socksreq[5] = 0;\n        socksreq[6] = 0;\n        socksreq[7] = 1;\n        /* append hostname */\n        hostnamelen = strlen(sx->hostname) + 1; /* length including NUL */\n        if(hostnamelen <= 255)\n          strcpy((char *)socksreq + packetsize, sx->hostname);\n        else {\n          failf(data, \"SOCKS4: too long host name\");\n          return CURLPX_LONG_HOSTNAME;\n        }\n        packetsize += hostnamelen;\n      }\n      sx->outp = socksreq;\n      sx->outstanding = packetsize;\n      sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_SENDING);\n    }\n    /* FALLTHROUGH */\n  case CONNECT_REQ_SENDING:\n    /* Send request */\n    presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_CONNECT,\n                               \"SOCKS4 connect request\");\n    if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n      return presult;\n    else if(sx->outstanding) {\n      /* remain in sending state */\n      return CURLPX_OK;\n    }\n    /* done sending! */\n    sx->outstanding = 8; /* receive data size */\n    sx->outp = socksreq;\n    sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_SOCKS_READ);\n\n    /* FALLTHROUGH */\n  case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ:\n    /* Receive response */\n    presult = socks_state_recv(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_RECV_CONNECT,\n                               \"connect request ack\");\n    if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n      return presult;\n    else if(sx->outstanding) {\n      /* remain in reading state */\n      return CURLPX_OK;\n    }\n    sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_DONE);\n    break;\n  default: /* lots of unused states in SOCKS4 */\n    break;\n  }\n\n  /*\n   * Response format\n   *\n   *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+\n   *     | VN | CD | DSTPORT |      DSTIP        |\n   *     +----+----+----+----+----+----+----+----+\n   * # of bytes:  1    1      2              4\n   *\n   * VN is the version of the reply code and should be 0. CD is the result\n   * code with one of the following values:\n   *\n   * 90: request granted\n   * 91: request rejected or failed\n   * 92: request rejected because SOCKS server cannot connect to\n   *     identd on the client\n   * 93: request rejected because the client program and identd\n   *     report different user-ids\n   */\n\n  /* wrong version ? */\n  if(socksreq[0]) {\n    failf(data,\n          \"SOCKS4 reply has wrong version, version should be 0.\");\n    return CURLPX_BAD_VERSION;\n  }\n\n  /* Result */\n  switch(socksreq[1]) {\n  case 90:\n    infof(data, \"SOCKS4%s request granted.\", protocol4a?\"a\":\"\");\n    break;\n  case 91:\n    failf(data,\n          \"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\"\n          \", request rejected or failed.\",\n          socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\n          (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\n          (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\n    return CURLPX_REQUEST_FAILED;\n  case 92:\n    failf(data,\n          \"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\"\n          \", request rejected because SOCKS server cannot connect to \"\n          \"identd on the client.\",\n          socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\n          (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\n          (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\n    return CURLPX_IDENTD;\n  case 93:\n    failf(data,\n          \"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\"\n          \", request rejected because the client program and identd \"\n          \"report different user-ids.\",\n          socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\n          (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\n          (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\n    return CURLPX_IDENTD_DIFFER;\n  default:\n    failf(data,\n          \"Can't complete SOCKS4 connection to %d.%d.%d.%d:%d. (%d)\"\n          \", Unknown.\",\n          socksreq[4], socksreq[5], socksreq[6], socksreq[7],\n          (((unsigned char)socksreq[2] << 8) | (unsigned char)socksreq[3]),\n          (unsigned char)socksreq[1]);\n    return CURLPX_UNKNOWN_FAIL;\n  }\n\n  return CURLPX_OK; /* Proxy was successful! */\n}\n\n/*\n * This function logs in to a SOCKS5 proxy and sends the specifics to the final\n * destination server.\n */\nstatic CURLproxycode do_SOCKS5(struct Curl_cfilter *cf,\n                               struct socks_state *sx,\n                               struct Curl_easy *data)\n{\n  /*\n    According to the RFC1928, section \"6.  Replies\". This is what a SOCK5\n    replies:\n\n        +----+-----+-------+------+----------+----------+\n        |VER | REP |  RSV  | ATYP | BND.ADDR | BND.PORT |\n        +----+-----+-------+------+----------+----------+\n        | 1  |  1  | X'00' |  1   | Variable |    2     |\n        +----+-----+-------+------+----------+----------+\n\n    Where:\n\n    o  VER    protocol version: X'05'\n    o  REP    Reply field:\n    o  X'00' succeeded\n  */\n  struct connectdata *conn = cf->conn;\n  unsigned char *socksreq = (unsigned char *)data->state.buffer;\n  int idx;\n  CURLcode result;\n  CURLproxycode presult;\n  bool socks5_resolve_local =\n    (conn->socks_proxy.proxytype == CURLPROXY_SOCKS5) ? TRUE : FALSE;\n  const size_t hostname_len = strlen(sx->hostname);\n  ssize_t len = 0;\n  const unsigned char auth = data->set.socks5auth;\n  bool allow_gssapi = FALSE;\n  struct Curl_dns_entry *dns = NULL;\n\n  DEBUGASSERT(auth & (CURLAUTH_BASIC | CURLAUTH_GSSAPI));\n  switch(sx->state) {\n  case CONNECT_SOCKS_INIT:\n    if(conn->bits.httpproxy)\n      infof(data, \"SOCKS5: connecting to HTTP proxy %s port %d\",\n            sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\n\n    /* RFC1928 chapter 5 specifies max 255 chars for domain name in packet */\n    if(!socks5_resolve_local && hostname_len > 255) {\n      infof(data, \"SOCKS5: server resolving disabled for hostnames of \"\n            \"length > 255 [actual len=%zu]\", hostname_len);\n      socks5_resolve_local = TRUE;\n    }\n\n    if(auth & ~(CURLAUTH_BASIC | CURLAUTH_GSSAPI))\n      infof(data,\n            \"warning: unsupported value passed to CURLOPT_SOCKS5_AUTH: %u\",\n            auth);\n    if(!(auth & CURLAUTH_BASIC))\n      /* disable username/password auth */\n      sx->proxy_user = NULL;\n#if defined(HAVE_GSSAPI) || defined(USE_WINDOWS_SSPI)\n    if(auth & CURLAUTH_GSSAPI)\n      allow_gssapi = TRUE;\n#endif\n\n    idx = 0;\n    socksreq[idx++] = 5;   /* version */\n    idx++;                 /* number of authentication methods */\n    socksreq[idx++] = 0;   /* no authentication */\n    if(allow_gssapi)\n      socksreq[idx++] = 1; /* GSS-API */\n    if(sx->proxy_user)\n      socksreq[idx++] = 2; /* username/password */\n    /* write the number of authentication methods */\n    socksreq[1] = (unsigned char) (idx - 2);\n\n    sx->outp = socksreq;\n    sx->outstanding = idx;\n    presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_CONNECT,\n                               \"initial SOCKS5 request\");\n    if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n      return presult;\n    else if(sx->outstanding) {\n      /* remain in sending state */\n      return CURLPX_OK;\n    }\n    sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_SOCKS_READ);\n    goto CONNECT_SOCKS_READ_INIT;\n  case CONNECT_SOCKS_SEND:\n    presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_CONNECT,\n                               \"initial SOCKS5 request\");\n    if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n      return presult;\n    else if(sx->outstanding) {\n      /* remain in sending state */\n      return CURLPX_OK;\n    }\n    /* FALLTHROUGH */\nCONNECT_SOCKS_READ_INIT:\n  case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ_INIT:\n    sx->outstanding = 2; /* expect two bytes */\n    sx->outp = socksreq; /* store it here */\n    /* FALLTHROUGH */\n  case CONNECT_SOCKS_READ:\n    presult = socks_state_recv(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_RECV_CONNECT,\n                               \"initial SOCKS5 response\");\n    if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n      return presult;\n    else if(sx->outstanding) {\n      /* remain in reading state */\n      return CURLPX_OK;\n    }\n    else if(socksreq[0] != 5) {\n      failf(data, \"Received invalid version in initial SOCKS5 response.\");\n      return CURLPX_BAD_VERSION;\n    }\n    else if(socksreq[1] == 0) {\n      /* DONE! No authentication needed. Send request. */\n      sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_INIT);\n      goto CONNECT_REQ_INIT;\n    }\n    else if(socksreq[1] == 2) {\n      /* regular name + password authentication */\n      sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_AUTH_INIT);\n      goto CONNECT_AUTH_INIT;\n    }\n#if defined(HAVE_GSSAPI) || defined(USE_WINDOWS_SSPI)\n    else if(allow_gssapi && (socksreq[1] == 1)) {\n      sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_GSSAPI_INIT);\n      result = Curl_SOCKS5_gssapi_negotiate(cf, data);\n      if(result) {\n        failf(data, \"Unable to negotiate SOCKS5 GSS-API context.\");\n        return CURLPX_GSSAPI;\n      }\n    }\n#endif\n    else {\n      /* error */\n      if(!allow_gssapi && (socksreq[1] == 1)) {\n        failf(data,\n              \"SOCKS5 GSSAPI per-message authentication is not supported.\");\n        return CURLPX_GSSAPI_PERMSG;\n      }\n      else if(socksreq[1] == 255) {\n        failf(data, \"No authentication method was acceptable.\");\n        return CURLPX_NO_AUTH;\n      }\n    }\n    failf(data,\n          \"Undocumented SOCKS5 mode attempted to be used by server.\");\n    return CURLPX_UNKNOWN_MODE;\n#if defined(HAVE_GSSAPI) || defined(USE_WINDOWS_SSPI)\n  case CONNECT_GSSAPI_INIT:\n    /* GSSAPI stuff done non-blocking */\n    break;\n#endif\n\n  default: /* do nothing! */\n    break;\n\nCONNECT_AUTH_INIT:\n  case CONNECT_AUTH_INIT: {\n    /* Needs user name and password */\n    size_t proxy_user_len, proxy_password_len;\n    if(sx->proxy_user && sx->proxy_password) {\n      proxy_user_len = strlen(sx->proxy_user);\n      proxy_password_len = strlen(sx->proxy_password);\n    }\n    else {\n      proxy_user_len = 0;\n      proxy_password_len = 0;\n    }\n\n    /*   username/password request looks like\n     * +----+------+----------+------+----------+\n     * |VER | ULEN |  UNAME   | PLEN |  PASSWD  |\n     * +----+------+----------+------+----------+\n     * | 1  |  1   | 1 to 255 |  1   | 1 to 255 |\n     * +----+------+----------+------+----------+\n     */\n    len = 0;\n    socksreq[len++] = 1;    /* username/pw subnegotiation version */\n    socksreq[len++] = (unsigned char) proxy_user_len;\n    if(sx->proxy_user && proxy_user_len) {\n      /* the length must fit in a single byte */\n      if(proxy_user_len > 255) {\n        failf(data, \"Excessive user name length for proxy auth\");\n        return CURLPX_LONG_USER;\n      }\n      memcpy(socksreq + len, sx->proxy_user, proxy_user_len);\n    }\n    len += proxy_user_len;\n    socksreq[len++] = (unsigned char) proxy_password_len;\n    if(sx->proxy_password && proxy_password_len) {\n      /* the length must fit in a single byte */\n      if(proxy_password_len > 255) {\n        failf(data, \"Excessive password length for proxy auth\");\n        return CURLPX_LONG_PASSWD;\n      }\n      memcpy(socksreq + len, sx->proxy_password, proxy_password_len);\n    }\n    len += proxy_password_len;\n    sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_AUTH_SEND);\n    sx->outstanding = len;\n    sx->outp = socksreq;\n  }\n    /* FALLTHROUGH */\n  case CONNECT_AUTH_SEND:\n    presult = socks_state_send(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_SEND_AUTH,\n                               \"SOCKS5 sub-negotiation request\");\n    if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n      return presult;\n    else if(sx->outstanding) {\n      /* remain in sending state */\n      return CURLPX_OK;\n    }\n    sx->outp = socksreq;\n    sx->outstanding = 2;\n    sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_AUTH_READ);\n    /* FALLTHROUGH */\n  case CONNECT_AUTH_READ:\n    presult = socks_state_recv(cf, sx, data, CURLPX_RECV_AUTH,\n                               \"SOCKS5 sub-negotiation response\");\n    if(CURLPX_OK != presult)\n      return presult;\n    else if(sx->outstanding) {\n      /* remain in reading state */\n      return CURLPX_OK;\n    }\n    /* ignore the first (VER) byte */\n    else if(socksreq[1]) { /* status */\n      failf(data, \"User was rejected by the SOCKS5 server (%d %d).\",\n            socksreq[0], socksreq[1]);\n      return CURLPX_USER_REJECTED;\n    }\n\n    /* Everything is good so far, user was authenticated! */\n    sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_INIT);\n    /* FALLTHROUGH */\nCONNECT_REQ_INIT:\n  case CONNECT_REQ_INIT:\n    if(socks5_resolve_local) {\n      enum resolve_t rc = Curl_resolv(data, sx->hostname, sx->remote_port,\n                                      TRUE, &dns);\n\n      if(rc == CURLRESOLV_ERROR)\n        return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\n\n      if(rc == CURLRESOLV_PENDING) {\n        sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVING);\n        return CURLPX_OK;\n      }\n      sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_RESOLVED);\n      goto CONNECT_RESOLVED;\n    }\n    goto CONNECT_RESOLVE_REMOTE;\n\n  case CONNECT_RESOLVING:\n    /* check if we have the name resolved by now */\n    dns = Curl_fetch_addr(data, sx->hostname, sx->remote_port);\n\n    if(dns) {\n#ifdef CURLRES_ASYNCH\n      data->state.async.dns = dns;\n      data->state.async.done = TRUE;\n#endif\n      infof(data, \"SOCKS5: hostname '%s' found\", sx->hostname);\n    }\n\n    if(!dns) {\n      result = Curl_resolv_check(data, &dns);\n      if(!dns) {\n        if(result)\n          return CURLPX_RESOLVE_HOST;\n        return CURLPX_OK;\n      }\n    }\n    /* FALLTHROUGH */\nCONNECT_RESOLVED:\n  case This is set from the user-provided hostname via the --proxy flag or API. The cast to `char` could be problematic if hostname_len > 255, as it would be truncated or wrapped around.\n\nHowever, looking at line 589:\n```c\nif(!socks5_resolve_local && hostname_len > 255) {\n  infof(data, \"SOCKS5: server resolving disabled for hostnames of \"\n        \"length > 255 [actual len=%zu]\", hostname_len);\n  socks5_resolve_local = TRUE;\n}\n```\n\nSo if the hostname is longer than 255 bytes, the code automatically switches to local resolution mode, which avoids this issue. This is a safety measure.\n\nNow let me analyze the real vulnerability. The most likely issue is in the parsing of the SOCKS5 server response at line 1005-1008:\n```c\nif(socksreq[3] == 3) {\n  /* domain name */\n  int addrlen = (int) socksreq[4];\n  len = 5 + addrlen + 2;\n}\n```\n\nThe problem is that `socksreq[4]` comes from the server response, and if the server is malicious or compromised, it can send an arbitrary value. If the ATYP is 3 (domain name) but the actual data sent is less than expected (or even non-existent), the code will try to read more data from the socket than is available, or it will use uninitialized memory.\n\nHowever, the code does handle this by using the `socks_state_recv()` function which reads `sx->outstanding` bytes. If fewer bytes are available, it will return CURLPX_OK and remain in the reading state. \n\nIf the connection drops, an error gets returned. But a malicious server could send a domain name length of 255 while only providing a few bytes of actual data, causing curl to hang waiting for the remaining bytes that never arrive. This would be a denial of service condition rather than code This function is directly reachable when:\n1. A user specifies a SOCKS5 proxy configuration via the `--proxy socks5://...` command-line flag or the `CURLOPT_PROXY` API\n2. The curl client attempts to establish a connection through the specified SOCKS5 proxy\n3. The SOCKS5 proxy server (which may be attacker-controlled) sends responses that are parsed by this function\n\nThe `do_SOCKS5()` function processes SOCKS5 proxy handshake and authentication, including parsing server responses that contain attacker-controlled data.\n\n---\n\n## Affected Code\n\n**Function**: `do_SOCKS5()`\n**File**: `/workspace/lib/socks.c:548-1054`\n**Description**:\n- Implements SOCKS5 proxy authentication and connection negotiation per RFC 1928\n- Handles the complete SOCKS5 handshake including:\n  - Initial protocol version negotiation\n  - Authentication method selection (none, username/password, or GSSAPI)\n  - Username/password authentication exchange\n  - Connection request to remote host\n  - Parsing of server responses (including variable-length address fields)\n- Processes responses from the SOCKS5 proxy server, which are potentially attacker-controlled\n\n---\n\n## Attack Path\n\n### Complete Call Chain\n\n```\ncurl_easy_perform() / curl_multi_perform()\n  ↓\nmulti_runsingle() [lib/multi.c:1868]\n  ↓\nCurl_connect() [lib/url.c:3895]\n  ↓\ncreate_conn() → Curl_setup_conn()\n  ↓\nCurl_conn_setup() [lib/connect.c]\n  ↓\ncf_setup_connect() [lib/connect.c:1186]\n  ↓\nCurl_cf_socks_proxy_insert_after() [lib/socks.c:1240]\n  ↓\nsocks_proxy_cf_connect() [lib/socks.c:1103]\n  ↓\nconnect_SOCKS() [lib/socks.c:1056]\n  ↓\ndo_SOCKS5() [lib/socks.c:548] ← VULNERABLE FUNCTION\n```\n\n### Function Roles in Call Chain\n\n1. **curl_easy_perform() / curl_multi_perform()** (user entry point)\n   - Main user-facing API that initiates the transfer\n   - User specifies proxy via `--proxy` flag or CURLOPT_PROXY option\n\n2. **multi_runsingle()** [lib/multi.c:1868]\n   - Main state machine for transfer operations\n   - Orchestrates connection establishment and protocol handling\n   - Calls `Curl_connect()` when in MSTATE_CONNECT state (line 1962)\n\n3. **Curl_connect()** [lib/url.c:3895]\n   - High-level connection coordinator\n   - Initiates connection setup via `Curl_setup_conn()`\n\n4. **Curl_conn_setup()** [lib/connect.c]\n   - Validates proxy configuration and DNS information\n   - Sets up filter chain for the connection\n\n5. **cf_setup_connect()** [lib/connect.c:1186]\n   - Connection filter setup state machine\n   - Determines which filters to insert based on proxy type\n   - **Key decision point** (line 1217): If `cf->conn->bits.socksproxy` is true, calls `Curl_cf_socks_proxy_insert_after()`\n\n6. **Curl_cf_socks_proxy_insert_after()** [lib/socks.c:1240]\n   - Creates and inserts the SOCKS proxy connection filter\n   - Allocates the socks_state structure\n\n7. **socks_proxy_cf_connect()** [lib/socks.c:1103]\n   - Connection filter's connect handler\n   - Initializes socks_state with target hostname and port\n   - **Key data sources** (line 1133-1146):\n     - `sx->hostname` ← User-provided hostname from HTTP/HTTPS request\n     - `sx->remote_port` ← User-provided port\n     - `sx->proxy_user` ← Proxy credentials from proxy URL\n     - `sx->proxy_password` ← Proxy credentials from proxy URL\n   - Calls `connect_SOCKS()` to perform SOCKS negotiation\n\n8. **connect_SOCKS()** [lib/socks.c:1056]\n   - Dispatcher function that routes to the appropriate SOCKS handler\n   - **Decision point** (line 1064-1073): Routes to `do_SOCKS5()` if proxy type is SOCKS5 or SOCKS5_HOSTNAME\n\n9. **do_SOCKS5()** [lib/socks.c:548] ← **VULNERABLE FUNCTION**\n   - Executes SOCKS5 protocol state machine\n   - **External input received here**:\n     - SOCKS5 server responses (lines 645-692): authentication method selection\n     - SOCKS5 server authentication challenge responses (line 762-776)\n     - SOCKS5 server connection response (line 951-1049): includes BND.ADDR field with variable length\n\n---\n\n## Severity Assessment\n\n### Reachability: YES - REACHABLE\n\n**Conditions for Reaching `do_SOCKS5()`:**\n\n1. **User Action**: User must specify a SOCKS5 proxy:\n   ```bash\n   curl https://example.com --proxy socks5://proxy.example.com:1080\n   # OR via API\n   curl_easy_setopt(handle, CURLOPT_PROXY, \"socks5://proxy.example.com:1080\");\n   ```\n\n2. **Network Condition**:\n   - The SOCKS5 proxy must be reachable from the client\n   - A TCP connection to the proxy's port must be established\n   - The proxy must respond with SOCKS5 protocol messages\n\n### Attack Vector\n\nAn attacker can trigger `do_SOCKS5()` execution by:\n\n1. **Controlling the SOCKS5 proxy server**\n   - Deploy a malicious SOCKS5 proxy on a network path\n   - Intercept traffic to a legitimate proxy (MITM attack)\n   - Compromise a legitimate proxy server\n\n2. **Social engineering**\n   - Trick users into configuring curl to use an attacker-controlled proxy\n   - Distribute scripts/configurations that specify malicious proxy\n\n3. **Supply chain compromise**\n   - Inject proxy configuration in shared scripts or deployment tools\n   - Modify environment variables or proxy auto-config (PAC) files\n\n### External Input Reaching `do_SOCKS5()`\n\nThe following data from the SOCKS5 proxy server reaches `do_SOCKS5()`:\n\n1. **Authentication Method Response** (line 645):\n   ```c\n   /* socksreq[1] contains the selected authentication method */\n   socksreq[0]  // Protocol version (expected: 5)\n   socksreq[1]  // Selected auth method (0, 1, 2, or 255)\n   ```\n   **Source**: Untrusted SOCKS5 server response\n   **Impact**: Determines authentication path; invalid values handled with error checks\n\n2. **Authentication Response** (line 762):\n   ```c\n   /* For username/password authentication */\n   socksreq[0]  // Subnegotiation version\n   socksreq[1]  // Status (0 = success, non-zero = failure)\n   ```\n   **Source**: Untrusted SOCKS5 server response\n   **Impact**: Determines if authentication succeeds; invalid responses cause connection termination\n\n3. **Connection Response - Variable Length Address** (line 1005-1020):\n server response (BND.ADDR field), specifically ATYP field\n   **Impact**: Determines how many bytes to read from the response stream\n   **Attacker Control**: Complete control over `socksreq[3]` and `socksreq[4]` values\n\n### Vulnerability Analysis\n\n**Potential Issue: Integer Overflow / Underflow**\n\nAt line 1007, the code casts an unsigned char to a signed int:\n```c\nint addrlen = (int) socksreq[4];  // socksreq[4] is unsigned char (0-255)\nlen = 5 + addrlen + 2;\n```\n\n**Assessment**: NOT VULNERABLE\n- `socksreq[4]` is an unsigned char, range 0-255\n- Casting to signed int cannot produce negative values\n- Maximum `len = 5 + 255 + 2 = 262 bytes`\n- Buffer (data->state.buffer) is guaranteed ≥ 1024 bytes (READBUFFER_MIN)\n- 262 bytes is well within buffer bounds\n\n**Potential Issue: Hostname Length Truncation**\n\nAt line 906, during remote resolution:\n```c\nsocksreq[len++] = (char) hostname_len;  /* one byte address length */\nmemcpy(&socksreq[len], sx->hostname, hostname_len);\n```\n\n**Assessment**: PROTECTED\n- Code explicitly checks for hostname_len > 255 at line 589:\n```c\nif(!socks5_resolve_local && hostname_len > 255) {\n  infof(data, \"SOCKS5: server resolving disabled for hostnames of \"\n        \"length > 255 [actual len=%zu]\", hostname_len);\n  socks5_resolve_local = TRUE;\n}\n```\n- If hostname exceeds 255 bytes, switches to local resolution to avoid this code path\n- No buffer overflow possible\n\n**Actual Issue: Denial of Service / Protocol Desynchronization**\n\nWhile not a code execution vulnerability, there is a potential DoS issue:\n\nAt lines 1027-1030:\n```c\nif(len > 10) {\n  sx->outstanding = len - 10;  /* bytes to read */\n  sx->outp = &socksreq[10];\n  sxstate(sx, data, CONNECT_REQ_READ_MORE);\n}\n```\n\nIf a malicious SOCKS5 server:\n1. Sends `socksreq[3] = 3` (domain name type)\n2. Sets `socksreq[4] = 255` (claim 255 bytes of domain)\n3. Only sends partial data (e.g., 5 bytes)\n4. Closes or stalls the connection\n\nThen curl would either:\n- **Hang indefinitely** waiting for 252 bytes that never arrive (socket timeout depending on curl settings)\n- **Or timeout** if a read timeout is configured\n\n**Impact**: Denial of Service (hang/timeout), not remote code execution\n\n---\n\n## Remediation\n\n### Current State: PARTIALLY MITIGATED\n\nThe code already includes some safety measures:\n\n1. **Hostname length validation** (line 589-592)\n   - Prevents truncation of long hostnames\n   - Switches to local resolution if hostname exceeds 255 bytes\n\n2. **Buffer size guarantee** (line 287)\n   - `DEBUGASSERT(READBUFFER_MIN >= 600)` ensures minimum 1024-byte buffer\n   - Maximum possible packet size (262 bytes) is well within bounds\n\n3. **Protocol validation** (line 654, 960-963)\n   - Validates SOCKS5 version field\n   - Returns error if version != 5\n\n### Recommended Additional Hardening\n\n**If code execution or memory corruption is the concern:**\n- Current mitigations appear adequate\n- The buffer size guarantee and hostname length check prevent overflow scenarios\n- The maximum address field length (255 bytes) is inherently bounded by SOCKS5 RFC 1928\n\n**If protocol robustness is the concern (prevent DoS/hang):**\n\n1. **Add maximum response packet size validation**:\n   ```c\n   /* Calculate real packet size */\n   if(socksreq[3] == 3) {\n     int addrlen = (int) socksreq[4];\n     len = 5 + addrlen + 2;\n     /* Verify length is reasonable (add bounds check) */\n     if(len > data->set.buffer_size) {\n       failf(data, \"SOCKS5 response packet too large\");\n       return CURLPX_GENERAL_SERVER_FAILURE;\n     }\n   }\n   ```\n\n2. **Add explicit timeout handling** for partial responses (already handled by curl's timeout system)\n\n3. **Add logging of suspicious responses**:\n   ```c\n   if(len > 100) {  /* arbitrary threshold */\n     infof(data, \"SOCKS5: large response size %zu (addrlen=%d)\", len, addrlen);\n   }\n   ```\n\n### Assessment Summary\n\n- **Buffer overflow**: NOT POSSIBLE - maximum response is 262 bytes, buffer is 1024+ bytes\n- **Integer overflow**: NOT POSSIBLE - unsigned char to int cast is safe\n- **Hostname truncation**: PROTECTED - code switches to local resolution for long hostnames\n- **Denial of Service**: POSSIBLE - malicious server can send truncated responses causing hang\n- **Remote Code Execution**: NOT POSSIBLE - no exploit path identified\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nThe `do_SOCKS5()` function is **REACHABLE from external input** when a user specifies a SOCKS5 proxy.
